## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    subgraph Input["Data Sources"]
        A1[Container Logs]
        A2[Host Logs]
        A3[System Logs]
        A4[Application Metrics]
        A5[GPU Metrics]
        A6[Neuron Metrics]
        A7[Application Traces]
    end
    
    subgraph Collectors["Collectors & Agents"]
        B1[Fluent Bit]
        B2[CloudWatch Agent]
        B3[DCGM Exporter]
        B4[Neuron Monitor]
    end
    
    subgraph Processing["Processing"]
        C1[Kubernetes Filter]
        C2[AWS Filter]
        C3[Parser]
        C4[Enhanced Container Insights]
        C5[Application Signals]
    end
    
    subgraph Output["AWS CloudWatch"]
        D1[CloudWatch Logs<br/>/application]
        D2[CloudWatch Logs<br/>/dataplane]
        D3[CloudWatch Logs<br/>/host]
        D4[CloudWatch Metrics]
        D5[CloudWatch Traces]
    end
    
    A1 --> B1
    A2 --> B1
    A3 --> B1
    B1 --> C1
    B1 --> C2
    B1 --> C3
    C1 --> D1
    C2 --> D2
    C3 --> D3
    
    A4 --> B2
    A7 --> B2
    B2 --> C4
    B2 --> C5
    C4 --> D4
    C5 --> D5
    
    A5 --> B3
    B3 --> B2
    
    A6 --> B4
    B4 --> B2
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
classDiagram
    class AmazonCloudWatchObservability {
        +String clusterName
        +String region
        +int replicaCount
        +List gpuInstances
        +List neuronInstances
        +tolerations
    }
    
    class Manager {
        +String image
        +String tag
        +Map autoInstrumentationImage
        +Map autoInstrumentationConfiguration
        +Resources resources
        +ServiceAccount serviceAccount
        +Map env
    }
    
    class ContainerLogs {
        +boolean enabled
        +FluentBit fluentBit
    }
    
    class FluentBit {
        +Image image
        +Resources resources
        +String priorityClassName
        +Config config
        +ConfigWindows configWindows
    }
    
    class Agent {
        +String name
        +String mode
        +int replicas
        +Image image
        +boolean enabled
        +String priorityClassName
        +Resources resources
        +Config config
        +DefaultConfig defaultConfig
        +Prometheus prometheus
    }
    
    class Prometheus {
        +Config config
        +TargetAllocator targetAllocator
    }
    
    class TargetAllocator {
        +boolean enabled
        +Image image
        +PrometheusCR prometheusCR
    }
    
    class DCGMExporter {
        +Image image
        +Resources resources
        +String configmap
        +List arguments
        +Service service
        +ServiceAccount serviceAccount
    }
    
    class NeuronMonitor {
        +Image image
        +Resources resources
        +String configmap
        +Service service
        +SecurityContext securityContext
        +ServiceAccount serviceAccount
    }
    
    class AdmissionWebhooks {
        +boolean create
        +String failurePolicy
        +String secretName
        +AutoGenerateCert autoGenerateCert
        +CertManager certManager
    }
    
    AmazonCloudWatchObservability --> Manager
    AmazonCloudWatchObservability --> ContainerLogs
    AmazonCloudWatchObservability --> Agent
    AmazonCloudWatchObservability --> DCGMExporter
    AmazonCloudWatchObservability --> NeuronMonitor
    AmazonCloudWatchObservability --> AdmissionWebhooks
    ContainerLogs --> FluentBit
    Agent --> Prometheus
    Prometheus --> TargetAllocator
```
